\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ header\ file\ defines\ abstractions\ for\ computing\ with\ absolute\ points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ in\ time,\ durations\ of\ time,\ and\ formatting\ and\ parsing\ time\ within\ a\ given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ time\ zone.\ The\ following\ abstractions\ are\ defined:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ *\ \`{}absl::Time`\ defines\ an\ absolute,\ specific\ instance\ in\ time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ *\ \`{}absl::Duration`\ defines\ a\ signed,\ fixed-\/length\ span\ of\ time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ *\ \`{}absl::TimeZone`\ defines\ geopolitical\ time\ zone\ regions\ (as\ collected}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ within\ the\ IANA\ Time\ Zone\ database\ (https://www.iana.org/time-\/zones)).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note:\ Absolute\ times\ are\ distinct\ from\ civil\ times,\ which\ refer\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ human-\/scale\ time\ commonly\ represented\ by\ \`{}YYYY-\/MM-\/DD\ hh:mm:ss`.\ The\ mapping}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ between\ absolute\ and\ civil\ times\ can\ be\ specified\ by\ use\ of\ time\ zones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (`absl::TimeZone`\ within\ this\ API).\ That\ is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Civil\ Time\ =\ F(Absolute\ Time,\ Time\ Zone)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Absolute\ Time\ =\ G(Civil\ Time,\ Time\ Zone)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ See\ civil\_time.h\ for\ abstractions\ related\ to\ constructing\ and\ manipulating}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ civil\ time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ absl::TimeZone\ nyc;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ //\ LoadTimeZone()\ may\ fail\ so\ it's\ always\ better\ to\ check\ for\ success.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ if\ (!absl::LoadTimeZone("{}America/New\_York"{},\ \&nyc))\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ //\ handle\ error\ case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00144\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Duration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00145\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00146\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ \`{}absl::Duration`\ class\ represents\ a\ signed,\ fixed-\/length\ amount\ of\ time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00147\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ \`{}Duration`\ is\ generated\ using\ a\ unit-\/specific\ factory\ function,\ or\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00148\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ result\ of\ subtracting\ one\ \`{}absl::Time`\ from\ another.\ Durations\ behave}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ like\ unit-\/safe\ integers\ and\ they\ support\ all\ the\ natural\ integer-\/like}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ arithmetic\ operations.\ Arithmetic\ overflows\ and\ saturates\ at\ +/-\/\ infinity.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}Duration`\ should\ be\ passed\ by\ value\ rather\ than\ const\ reference.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00152\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00153\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Factory\ functions\ \`{}Nanoseconds()`,\ \`{}Microseconds()`,\ \`{}Milliseconds()`,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00154\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}Seconds()`,\ \`{}Minutes()`,\ \`{}Hours()`\ and\ \`{}InfiniteDuration()`\ allow\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00155\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ creation\ of\ constexpr\ \`{}Duration`\ values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00156\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00157\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Examples:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00158\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00159\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ constexpr\ absl::Duration\ ten\_ns\ =\ absl::Nanoseconds(10);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00160\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ constexpr\ absl::Duration\ min\ =\ absl::Minutes(1);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00161\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ constexpr\ absl::Duration\ hour\ =\ absl::Hours(1);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00162\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ absl::Duration\ dur\ =\ 60\ *\ min;\ \ //\ dur\ ==\ hour}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00163\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ absl::Duration\ half\_sec\ =\ absl::Milliseconds(500);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00164\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ absl::Duration\ quarter\_sec\ =\ 0.25\ *\ absl::Seconds(1);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00165\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00166\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}Duration`\ values\ can\ be\ easily\ converted\ to\ an\ integral\ number\ of\ units}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00167\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ using\ the\ division\ operator.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00168\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00169\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00170\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00171\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ constexpr\ absl::Duration\ dur\ =\ absl::Milliseconds(1500);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00172\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ int64\_t\ ns\ =\ dur\ /\ absl::Nanoseconds(1);\ \ \ //\ ns\ ==\ 1500000000}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00173\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ int64\_t\ ms\ =\ dur\ /\ absl::Milliseconds(1);\ \ //\ ms\ ==\ 1500}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00174\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ int64\_t\ sec\ =\ dur\ /\ absl::Seconds(1);\ \ \ \ //\ sec\ ==\ 1\ (subseconds\ truncated)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00365\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ IDivDuration()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00366\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00367\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Divides\ a\ numerator\ \`{}Duration`\ by\ a\ denominator\ \`{}Duration`,\ returning\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00368\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ quotient\ and\ remainder.\ The\ remainder\ always\ has\ the\ same\ sign\ as\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00369\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ numerator.\ The\ returned\ quotient\ and\ remainder\ respect\ the\ identity:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00370\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00371\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ numerator\ =\ denominator\ *\ quotient\ +\ remainder}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00372\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00373\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Returned\ quotients\ are\ capped\ to\ the\ range\ of\ \`{}int64\_t`,\ with\ the\ difference}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00374\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ spilling\ into\ the\ remainder\ to\ uphold\ the\ above\ identity.\ This\ means\ that\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00375\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ remainder\ returned\ could\ differ\ from\ the\ remainder\ returned\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00376\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}Duration::operator\%`\ for\ huge\ quotients.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00377\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00378\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ See\ also\ the\ notes\ on\ \`{}InfiniteDuration()`\ below\ regarding\ the\ behavior\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00379\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ division\ involving\ zero\ and\ infinite\ durations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00380\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00381\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00382\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00383\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ constexpr\ absl::Duration\ a\ =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00384\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ absl::Seconds(std::numeric\_limits<int64\_t>::max());\ \ //\ big}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00385\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ constexpr\ absl::Duration\ b\ =\ absl::Nanoseconds(1);\ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ small}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00386\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00387\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ absl::Duration\ rem\ =\ a\ \%\ b;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00388\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ //\ rem\ ==\ absl::ZeroDuration()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00389\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00390\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ //\ Here,\ q\ would\ overflow\ int64\_t,\ so\ rem\ accounts\ for\ the\ difference.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00391\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ int64\_t\ q\ =\ absl::IDivDuration(a,\ b,\ \&rem);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00392\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ //\ q\ ==\ std::numeric\_limits<int64\_t>::max(),\ rem\ ==\ a\ -\/\ b\ *\ q}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00484\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00485\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Duration\ arithmetic\ overflows\ to\ +/-\/\ infinity\ and\ saturates.\ In\ general,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00486\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ arithmetic\ with\ \`{}Duration`\ infinities\ is\ similar\ to\ IEEE\ 754\ infinities}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00487\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ except\ where\ IEEE\ 754\ NaN\ would\ be\ involved,\ in\ which\ case\ +/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00488\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}InfiniteDuration()`\ is\ used\ in\ place\ of\ a\ "{}nan"{}\ Duration.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00489\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00745\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00746\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00747\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ An\ \`{}absl::Time`\ represents\ a\ specific\ instant\ in\ time.\ Arithmetic\ operators}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00748\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ are\ provided\ for\ naturally\ expressing\ time\ calculations.\ Instances\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00749\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ created\ using\ \`{}absl::Now()`\ and\ the\ \`{}absl::From*()`\ factory\ functions\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00750\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ accept\ the\ gamut\ of\ other\ time\ representations.\ Formatting\ and\ parsing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00751\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ functions\ are\ provided\ for\ conversion\ to\ and\ from\ strings.\ \ \`{}absl::Time`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00752\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ should\ be\ passed\ by\ value\ rather\ than\ const\ reference.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00753\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00754\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}absl::Time`\ assumes\ there\ are\ 60\ seconds\ in\ a\ minute,\ which\ means\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00755\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ underlying\ time\ scales\ must\ be\ "{}smeared"{}\ to\ eliminate\ leap\ seconds.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00756\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ See\ https://developers.google.com/time/smear.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00757\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00758\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Even\ though\ \`{}absl::Time`\ supports\ a\ wide\ range\ of\ timestamps,\ exercise}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00759\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ caution\ when\ using\ values\ in\ the\ distant\ past.\ \`{}absl::Time`\ uses\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00760\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Proleptic\ Gregorian\ calendar,\ which\ extends\ the\ Gregorian\ calendar\ backward}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00761\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ dates\ before\ its\ introduction\ in\ 1582.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00762\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ See\ https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proleptic\_Gregorian\_calendar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00763\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ for\ more\ information.\ Use\ the\ ICU\ calendar\ classes\ to\ convert\ a\ date\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00764\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ some\ other\ calendar\ (http://userguide.icu-\/project.org/datetime/calendar).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00765\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00766\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Similarly,\ standardized\ time\ zones\ are\ a\ reasonably\ recent\ innovation,\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00767\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ Greenwich\ prime\ meridian\ being\ established\ in\ 1884.\ The\ TZ\ database}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00768\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ itself\ does\ not\ profess\ accurate\ offsets\ for\ timestamps\ prior\ to\ 1970.\ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00769\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ breakdown\ of\ future\ timestamps\ is\ subject\ to\ the\ whim\ of\ regional}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00770\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ governments.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00771\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00772\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ \`{}absl::Time`\ class\ represents\ an\ instant\ in\ time\ as\ a\ count\ of\ clock}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00773\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ticks\ of\ some\ granularity\ (resolution)\ from\ some\ starting\ point\ (epoch).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00774\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00775\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}absl::Time`\ uses\ a\ resolution\ that\ is\ high\ enough\ to\ avoid\ loss\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00776\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ precision,\ and\ a\ range\ that\ is\ wide\ enough\ to\ avoid\ overflow,\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00777\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ converting\ between\ tick\ counts\ in\ most\ Google\ time\ scales\ (i.e.,\ resolution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00778\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ of\ at\ least\ one\ nanosecond,\ and\ range\ +/-\/100\ billion\ years).\ \ Conversions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00779\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ between\ the\ time\ scales\ are\ performed\ by\ truncating\ (towards\ negative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00780\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ infinity)\ to\ the\ nearest\ representable\ point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00781\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01072\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01073\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ \`{}absl::TimeZone`\ is\ an\ opaque,\ small,\ value-\/type\ class\ representing\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01074\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ geo-\/political\ region\ within\ which\ particular\ rules\ are\ used\ for\ converting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01075\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ between\ absolute\ and\ civil\ times\ (see\ https://git.io/v59Ly).\ \`{}absl::TimeZone`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01076\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ values\ are\ named\ using\ the\ TZ\ identifiers\ from\ the\ IANA\ Time\ Zone\ Database,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01077\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ such\ as\ "{}America/Los\_Angeles"{}\ or\ "{}Australia/Sydney"{}.\ \`{}absl::TimeZone`\ values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01078\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ are\ created\ from\ factory\ functions\ such\ as\ \`{}absl::LoadTimeZone()`.\ Note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01079\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ strings\ like\ "{}PST"{}\ and\ "{}EDT"{}\ are\ not\ valid\ TZ\ identifiers.\ Prefer\ to\ pass\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01080\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ value\ rather\ than\ const\ reference.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01081\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01153\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ It\ is\ possible\ for\ a\ caller\ to\ pass\ a\ civil-\/time\ value\ that\ does}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01154\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ not\ represent\ an\ actual\ or\ unique\ instant\ in\ time\ (due\ to\ a\ shift}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01156\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ civil-\/time\ components).\ For\ example,\ a\ daylight-\/saving-\/time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01157\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ transition\ skips\ or\ repeats\ civil\ times-\/-\/-\/in\ the\ United\ States,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01158\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ March\ 13,\ 2011\ 02:15\ never\ occurred,\ while\ November\ 6,\ 2011\ 01:15}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01159\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ occurred\ twice-\/-\/-\/so\ requests\ for\ such\ times\ are\ not\ well-\/defined.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01160\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ To\ account\ for\ these\ possibilities,\ \`{}absl::TimeZone::TimeInfo`\ is}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01469\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Formats\ the\ given\ \`{}absl::Time`\ in\ the\ \`{}absl::TimeZone`\ according\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01470\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ provided\ format\ string.\ Uses\ strftime()-\/like\ formatting\ options,\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01471\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ following\ extensions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01472\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01473\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ \%Ez\ \ -\/\ RFC3339-\/compatible\ numeric\ UTC\ offset\ (+hh:mm\ or\ -\/hh:mm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01474\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ \%E*z\ -\/\ Full-\/resolution\ numeric\ UTC\ offset\ (+hh:mm:ss\ or\ -\/hh:mm:ss)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01475\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ \%E\#S\ -\/\ Seconds\ with\ \#\ digits\ of\ fractional\ precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01476\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ \%E*S\ -\/\ Seconds\ with\ full\ fractional\ precision\ (a\ literal\ '*')}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01477\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ \%E\#f\ -\/\ Fractional\ seconds\ with\ \#\ digits\ of\ precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01478\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ \%E*f\ -\/\ Fractional\ seconds\ with\ full\ precision\ (a\ literal\ '*')}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01479\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ \%E4Y\ -\/\ Four-\/character\ years\ (-\/999\ ...\ -\/001,\ 0000,\ 0001\ ...\ 9999)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01480\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ \%ET\ \ -\/\ The\ RFC3339\ "{}date-\/time"{}\ separator\ "{}T"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01481\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01482\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note\ that\ \%E0S\ behaves\ like\ \%S,\ and\ \%E0f\ produces\ no\ characters.\ \ In}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01483\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ contrast\ \%E*f\ always\ produces\ at\ least\ one\ digit,\ which\ may\ be\ '0'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01484\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01485\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note\ that\ \%Y\ produces\ as\ many\ characters\ as\ it\ takes\ to\ fully\ render\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01486\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ year.\ \ A\ year\ outside\ of\ [-\/999:9999]\ when\ formatted\ with\ \%E4Y\ will\ produce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01487\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ more\ than\ four\ characters,\ just\ like\ \%Y.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01488\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01489\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ recommend\ that\ format\ strings\ include\ the\ UTC\ offset\ (\%z,\ \%Ez,\ or\ \%E*z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01490\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ so\ that\ the\ result\ uniquely\ identifies\ a\ time\ instant.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01491\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01492\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01493\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01524\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ParseTime()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01525\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01526\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Parses\ an\ input\ string\ according\ to\ the\ provided\ format\ string\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01527\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ returns\ the\ corresponding\ \`{}absl::Time`.\ Uses\ strftime()-\/like\ formatting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01528\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ options,\ with\ the\ same\ extensions\ as\ FormatTime(),\ but\ with\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01529\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ exceptions\ that\ \%E\#S\ is\ interpreted\ as\ \%E*S,\ and\ \%E\#f\ as\ \%E*f.\ \ \%Ez}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01530\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ \%E*z\ also\ accept\ the\ same\ inputs,\ which\ (along\ with\ \%z)\ includes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01531\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 'z'\ and\ 'Z'\ as\ synonyms\ for\ +00:00.\ \ \%ET\ accepts\ either\ 'T'\ or\ 't'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01532\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01533\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \%Y\ consumes\ as\ many\ numeric\ characters\ as\ it\ can,\ so\ the\ matching\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01534\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ should\ always\ be\ terminated\ with\ a\ non-\/numeric.\ \ \%E4Y\ always\ consumes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01535\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ exactly\ four\ characters,\ including\ any\ sign.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01536\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01537\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Unspecified\ fields\ are\ taken\ from\ the\ default\ date\ and\ time\ of\ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01538\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01539\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ "{}1970-\/01-\/01\ 00:00:00.0\ +0000"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01540\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01541\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ For\ example,\ parsing\ a\ string\ of\ "{}15:45"{}\ (\%H:\%M)\ will\ return\ an\ absl::Time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01542\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ that\ represents\ "{}1970-\/01-\/01\ 15:45:00.0\ +0000"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01543\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01544\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note\ that\ since\ ParseTime()\ returns\ time\ instants,\ it\ makes\ the\ most\ sense}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01545\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ parse\ fully-\/specified\ date/time\ strings\ that\ include\ a\ UTC\ offset\ (\%z,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01546\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \%Ez,\ or\ \%E*z).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01547\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01548\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note\ also\ that\ \`{}absl::ParseTime()`\ only\ heeds\ the\ fields\ year,\ month,\ day,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01549\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ hour,\ minute,\ (fractional)\ second,\ and\ UTC\ offset.\ \ Other\ fields,\ like}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01550\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ weekday\ (\%a\ or\ \%A),\ while\ parsed\ for\ syntactic\ validity,\ are\ ignored}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01551\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ in\ the\ conversion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01552\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01553\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Date\ and\ time\ fields\ that\ are\ out-\/of-\/range\ will\ be\ treated\ as\ errors}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01554\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ rather\ than\ normalizing\ them\ like\ \`{}absl::CivilSecond`\ does.\ \ For\ example,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01555\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ it\ is\ an\ error\ to\ parse\ the\ date\ "{}Oct\ 32,\ 2013"{}\ because\ 32\ is\ out\ of\ range.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01556\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01557\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ leap\ second\ of\ "{}:60"{}\ is\ normalized\ to\ "{}:00"{}\ of\ the\ following\ minute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01558\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ with\ fractional\ seconds\ discarded.\ \ The\ following\ table\ shows\ how\ the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01563\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ "{}00.x"{}\ -\/>\ 00.x\ \ //\ exact}}
